{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01SnpRRkShB684KrKwrGWip7","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→# APB Testbench Guide
for AI Agents\n     2→\n     3→This guide explains how to create UVM sequences for the APB testbench.\n     4→\n     5→## Repository Structure\n     6→\n     7→
```\n     8→repo/\n     9→├── src/hvl_top/test/sequences/\n    10→│   ├── master_sequences/          # Master agent sequences\n    11→│   │   ├── apb_master_bas
e_seq.sv # Base class for all master sequences\n    12→│   │   └── apb_master_seq_pkg.sv  # Package file - must include all sequences\n    13→│   └── slave_sequ
ences/           # Slave agent sequences (similar structure)\n    14→└── sim/cadence_sim/               # Simulation makefiles\n    15→```\n    16→\n    17→## C
reating a New Master Sequence\n    18→\n    19→### 1. Create the Sequence File\n    20→\n    21→File location: `repo/src/hvl_top/test/sequences/master_sequences
/apb_master_<name>_seq.sv`\n    22→\n    23→### 2. Implement the Sequence Class\n    24→\n    25→Your sequence must:\n    26→- Extend `apb_master_base_seq`\n
 27→- Include `uvm_object_utils` macro\n    28→- Implement a constructor that calls `super.new(name)`\n    29→- Implement a `body()` task\n    30→\n    31→### 3
. Implement the body() Task\n    32→\n    33→The body() task creates and sends transactions to the driver:\n    34→\n    35→```systemverilog\n    36→task body()
;\n    37→  // 1. Create transaction using UVM factory\n    38→  req = apb_master_tx::type_id::create(\"req\");\n    39→  \n    40→  // 2. Wait for sequencer to
 be ready\n    41→  start_item(req);\n    42→  \n    43→  // 3. Randomize with constraints\n    44→  assert(req.randomize() with {\n    45→    field1 == VALUE1;
\n    46→    field2 == VALUE2;\n    47→  });\n    48→  \n    49→  // 4. Set configuration handle\n    50→  req.apb_master_agent_cfg_h = p_sequencer.apb_master_a
gent_cfg_h;\n    51→  \n    52→  // 5. Send to driver\n    53→  finish_item(req);\n    54→endtask\n    55→```\n    56→\n    57→**Important:** `start_item()` mus
t be called before randomization and `finish_item()` must be called after.\n    58→\n    59→### 4. Add to Package File\n    60→\n    61→Edit `repo/src/hvl_top/t
est/sequences/master_sequences/apb_master_seq_pkg.sv`:\n    62→\n    63→```systemverilog\n    64→package apb_master_seq_pkg;\n    65→  // ... existing imports .
..\n    66→  \n    67→  `include \"apb_master_base_seq.sv\"\n    68→  `include \"apb_master_your_new_seq.sv\"  // ADD THIS LINE\n    69→  \n    70→endpackage :
apb_master_seq_pkg\n    71→```\n    72→\n    73→## APB Transaction Fields\n    74→\n    75→The `apb_master_tx` transaction has these key fields:\n    76→\n    7
7→- **`pwrite`**: Operation type - `WRITE` or `READ`\n    78→- **`transfer_size`**: Data width - `BIT_8`, `BIT_16`, `BIT_24`, or `BIT_32`\n    79→- **`pselx`**:
 Slave selection - `SLAVE_0`, `SLAVE_1`, etc.\n    80→- **`paddr`**: Address (randomized by default)\n    81→- **`pwdata`**: Write data (randomized by default)\
n    82→\n    83→## Common Constraint Patterns\n    84→\n    85→### Fixed transfer size and operation:\n    86→```systemverilog\n    87→assert(req.randomize() w
ith {\n    88→  transfer_size == BIT_8;\n    89→  pwrite == WRITE;\n    90→});\n    91→```\n    92→\n    93→### Specific slave:\n    94→```systemverilog\n    95
→assert(req.randomize() with {\n    96→  pselx == SLAVE_0;\n    97→});\n    98→```\n    99→\n   100→## UVM Factory Pattern\n   101→\n   102→Always use `type_id:
:create()` to instantiate objects:\n   103→```systemverilog\n   104→req = apb_master_tx::type_id::create(\"req\");\n   105→```\n   106→\n   107→This enables UVM
 factory overrides for better reusability.\n   108→\n   109→## Configuration Objects\n   110→\n   111→Sequences receive configuration from the sequencer via `p_
sequencer.apb_master_agent_cfg_h`. Always pass this to your transactions:\n   112→```systemverilog\n   113→req.apb_master_agent_cfg_h = p_sequencer.apb_master_a
gent_cfg_h;\n   114→```\n   115→\n   116→## Running Simulations\n   117→\n   118→From `repo/sim/cadence_sim/`:\n   119→```bash\n   120→make simulate TEST=apb_8b
_write_test\n   121→```\n   122→\n   123→This will:\n   124→1. Compile the testbench\n   125→2. Run the simulation\n   126→3. Generate coverage data\n   127→4.
Create log files in the test folder\n   128→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. You CAN

APB4 Protocol\n     2→\n     3→The idea of using Accelerated VIP is to push the synthesizable part of the testbench into the separate top module along with the
interface and it is named as HDL TOP and the unsynthesizable part is pushed into the HVL TOP. This setup provides the ability to run the longer tests quickly. T
his particular testbench can be used for the simulation as well as the emulation based on mode of operation.\n     4→\n     5→# Key Features  \n     6→1. It sup
ports addresses up to 32 bit wide.\n     7→2. APB4 support for write strobe signal to enable sparse data transfer on the write data bus.  \n     8→3. Single Mas
ter - Multiple Slaves.\n     9→4. Programmable Wait state insertion. \n    10→5. Slave supports fine grain control of response per address or per transfer.\n
 11→6. Programmable character length(multiple of 8 bits).\n    12→7. Supports protected access.\n    13→8. Random PSLVERR insertion.\n    14→9. Supports sending
